msg:I haven't written a review for a long time. This hotel must be rated 5 stars! The hotel supervisor Xiao Li is professional and enthusiastic. I won't say much about the routine operations of five-star hotels such as moving luggage and welcoming fruits. After learning that my wife had her birthday during her stay, she also helped me apply for a room upgrade. I was touched! We stayed for two days, and the service throughout the process was really amazing. The hotel is divided into three hotels: "Meng", "Ji" and "Zhong". Each hotel has distinct characteristics and meets the preferences of different groups of people. If you stay in any one of them, you can go to the other two hotels to take pictures, rest, etc. The hotel supplies are luxurious! Evian's mineral water, NFC's juice, Bulgari's toiletries, and especially need to say that the toothbrush is the most comfortable in all the hotels I have stayed in... But the most luxurious thing is the view of the room. Responsibly speaking-it's better than the observation deck! How pleasant it is to enjoy the most beautiful scenery of the scenic area while lying on the bed. Only those who have lived there can experience it. In short, this is one, no, three hotels that can add points to the journey. I recommend it to all friends who come to Xijiang Qianhu Miao Village. I wrote so much without realizing it, so I'll post photos!
